commit cccf637aca2926a6c74d726baff3a1f6723f7fa7
Merge: 7b5423a 48052fc
Author: Miquel Torres <tobami@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-12-31 12:19:11 +0000

    Merge pull request #233 from smarr/fixes/timeline-freeze-on-missing-data
    
    Ensure missing data points don’t lead to infinite loop

commit 48052fc011d57246cdc9a172d01669d716c66017
Author: Stefan Marr <git@stefan-marr.de>
Date:   2017-12-29 00:51:34 +0100

    Ensure missing data points don’t lead to infinite loop
    
    Missing data points can be represented as -1 values.
    For the timeline, this would mean we end up in an infinite loop, because the value would be always become smaller instead of bigger as it would be expected.
    
    This is avoided in two ways:
    - extract method determineSignificantDigits(.,.), which ensures the input value is positive
    - filter out negative numbers directly when collecting smallestValue
    
    Signed-off-by: Stefan Marr <git@stefan-marr.de>

20	10	codespeed/static/js/timeline.js

commit 7affd83c9c0e9ce4c266e9b383474c165962b64e
Author: Catalin Gabriel Manciu <catalin.gabriel.manciu@intel.com>
Date:   2016-11-29 15:11:24 +0200

    Add the 'makeimage' service
    
    This adds a service for generating chart images based on the latest
    benchmark results using the matplotlib module.
    The URL for this service is /sample_project/makeimage/.
    The image can be directly embedded in any HTML document using
    <img src="host_name/sample_project/makeimage/?...> or simply accessed
    using the same URL.
    
    The mandatory GET params are:
    env -   the environment's name
    proj -  the project's name
    branch -the branch's name
    exe -   the executable's name
    ben -   the benchmark's name
    The following params are optional:
    revs -  positive integer, number of results the image will display.
            revs=10 is the implicit value representing that the latest 10
            results will be displayed on the chart
    relative - if '1' or 'yes', instead of displaying absolute values,
            the first value from the series is used as a baseline and
            the chart will display percentual increments from that baseline
    base_commit - specifies a commit name to be used as a baseline instead
            of the first value of the series
    base_env - the environment's name to be used for the base_commit instead
            of env
    base_proj - the project's name to be used for the base_commit instead
            of proj
    base_exe - the executable's name to be use for the base_commit instead of
            exe

1	0	codespeed/urls.py
245	1	codespeed/views.py
1	0	requirements.txt

Merge: 977a54c aea70a2
Author: Miquel Torres <tobami@gmail.com>

commit aea70a22910d1d33c985c1c1d6b8c00bab500257
Author: Clément MATHIEU <clement@unportant.info>
Date:   2013-12-08 17:56:59 +0100

    Better SVN error message.
    
    Error messages reported by Pysvn are usually quite good. They easily allow to
    understand the issue and then fix it. Codespeed swallows this nice error message
    to replace it by a generic one hiding what was wrong.
    
    For example is anonymous users are not allowed, you will never be able to figure
    it out with the "Could not resolve" message.
    
    It seems better to expose the reported error as is rather than trying to "improve"
    it.

2	3	codespeed/subversion.py

commit d3a6043ec430af5ef4ba8ee1bba4a972b27d4fa6
Author: Frank Becker <fb@alien8.de>
Date:   2012-08-14 14:41:46 +0200

    add hierarchy to Benchmark model
    
        - Sometimes benchmarks have a big number of single results. It is
          favourable to keep them all. Thus, they might be organised in an
          hierarchical way.
          Example: To evaluate computer systems there might be one
          overall benchmark number. That number is calculated from sub
          benchmarks as CPU, hard disc I/O, RAM I/O, etc.
        - The single or the summarised result may be shown in the standard
          templates in a later version. For now all benchmarks are shown.
    
    Change-Id: I47062535bc0ec6e1d25ae857b4af74f207737c37

commit d4ce66e266f7d4a6b54834ff9f454856cf99d484
Author: Reiner Gerecke <mr.squidd@gmail.com>
Date:   2011-12-03 18:38:15 +0100

    Link revisions on changes page, #35
    
    The `commit_browsing_url` setting on a project allows to set a URL
    that will be used to link revisions on the changes page. Placeholders
    like {commitid} will be replaced by the appropriate information from the
    change log.
    
    Examples:
    
    https://github.com/tobami/codespeed/commit/{commitid}
    https://bitbucket.org/pypy/pypy/changeset/{commitid}

commit ec9cd1b6ebca6e031ee1ecbfc2b147f26d5799c6
Author: Reiner Gerecke <mr.squidd@gmail.com>
Date:   2011-12-18 13:53:53 +0100

    Load CSS in head, JavaScript at the end of the body
    
    Putting CSS in the head allows the page to render progressivly.
    Loading JavaScript in the head will block the download of other assets
    like images and css, therefore it should be put at the end of the
    document.
    
    See http://developer.yahoo.com/performance/rules.html

commit 677e1c1e5f5ece308eb74ea385fd76f961851a0a
Author: Reiner Gerecke <mr.squidd@gmail.com>
Date:   2011-12-09 14:27:54 +0100

    Reduce query count in getcomparisondata
    
    Benchmarks and environments don't have to be queried inside the loop,
    query them once outside.
    Also don't retrieve benchmark results one by one, but get them all for a
    specific revision/environment/executable combination.
    
    For the testdata fixture, this decreases query count from 47 to 24
    queries. With data from speed.pypy.org query count goes from 1893
    queries down to 75. Instead of 2.8s processing time, the data is
    collected in 100ms. Measured on SQLite, but other databases should
    benefit too.

    Configure what benchmarks are checked by default on comparison, #33
    
    Adds a new field to the Benchmark model that decides whether a benchmark
    is checked by default on the comparison page. Only on cross-project
    benchmarks can this field be true, an validation error will be raised
    otherwise.
    The included migration sets the field true for all cross-project
    benchmarks to keep current behaviour.

commit bebbe627fdd7e50ff1a099b2b54600870416fd0c
Author: Reiner Gerecke <mr.squidd@gmail.com>
Date:   2011-12-09 11:21:12 +0100

    Reduce database queries in getbaselineexecutables
    
    For every tagged revision found, another 3 queries were executed. Two to
    lookup branch.project and another one to find executables for that
    project. In total that is 1 + 3*(revision count) queries.
    
    This change uses select_related to prefetch branch.project and also
    prefetches all Executables, making it 2 queries total (when there are
    any revisions).
    
    Query count comparision:
    
    Revision count       Before      After
                 0            1          1
                 1            4          2
                10           31          2

commit 1b79120b30cc74df1373320f6187e8d3898f98f9
Author: Frank Becker <fb@alien8.de>
Date:   2011-08-12 00:42:37 +0200

    Fix lookup of Revisions() in displaylogs()
    
        - views.displaylogs() looks for the oldest rev of the rev.branch.
          Bug was that the filter looked for branch=rev.branch.project. Thus,
          the look up was Branch.objects.get(pk=rev.branch.project).
          It has to be Branch.objects.get(pk=rev.branch).
    
    Signed-off-by: Frank Becker <fb@alien8.de>

commit c4b7e50ec7b5cf7da3d11147942b2c343fa0b835
Author: Stefan Marr <git@stefan-marr.de>
Date:   2011-07-03 20:41:39 +0200

    Fixed the rendering of multiple executables for equidistant plots
    
    - updated the categoryAxisRenderer plugin to the latest version
      - this one includes an option for sorting the merged labels
      - however, it was broken :( reported the bug upstream and applied a fix to the minimized version used here
        (https://bitbucket.org/cleonello/jqplot/issue/375/categoryaxisrenderer-sortmergedlabels-does)
      - the non-minimized version looks like this:
     `if (isMerged && this.sortMergedLabels) {
        if (typeof labels[0] == "string") {
            labels.sort();
        } else {
            labels.sort(function(a,b) { return a - b; });
        }
    }`
     Will properly work for string labels, not sure for anything else than strings and numbers.
    
    - also added explicit sorting like done for https://github.com/tobami/codespeed/pull/46
      - this should be properly merged/replaced by the code from this pull request on integration
      - replacing is ok, since #46 only adds filtering on top
      - another option would be to do the sorting on the server and deliver already sorted data
    
    Signed-off-by: Stefan Marr <git@stefan-marr.de>

commit c01f776d9938f31cabcd0bb5ce55ba3df1f87c93
Author: daniloaf <daniloaf@ubuntu.(none)>
Date:   2011-05-04 19:40:04 -0300

    Adding two scripts to migrate old data.db to work with new Codespeed features.
    pypy_create_branches.py is a specific pypy data.db one, to create 2 trunk branches for PyPy and CPython projects
    migrate_script.py is a general one. It should be user only after user created all trunk branches for all projects.
    
    Follow these steps to migrate your data.db:
    $ python manage.py syncdb
    $ python manage.py migrate codespeed --fake
    $ python manage.py migrate codespeed
    $ python migrate_script.py
    
    Now, your data.db should be migrated :)
